```typescript
// utils/fetchRepoData.ts
import { readFileSync } from 'fs';
import { env } from 'process';

/**
 * Fetches repository data with strict error handling.
 * Returns a typed result or throws a descriptive error.
 */
export async function fetchRepoData(repoId: string): Promise<RepoInfo> {
  const apiKey = env.REPO_API_KEY;
  if (!apiKey) {
    throw new Error('Missing REPO_API_KEY environment variable');
  }

  const url = `https://api.example.com/repos/${repoId}`;
  const response = await fetch(url, {
    headers: {
      Authorization: `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
      // Ensure no accidental hard‑coded keys are sent
      'X-No-Hardcoded-Key': 'true',
    },
  });

  if (!response.ok) {
    // Defensive Execution: explicit else + error handling
    const errorBody = await response.text();
    throw new Error(`API request failed (${response.status}): ${errorBody}`);
  }

  const data = await response.json();
  // Simple data shape – no deep nesting, aligns with Pike’s Rule 3
  return {
    id: data.id,
    name: data.name,
    description: data.description,
  } as RepoInfo;
}

// utils/validator.ts
/**
 * Validates user input against the expected schema.
 * Returns a typed validation result.
 */
export function validateUserInput(input: unknown): { valid: true } | { valid: false; errors: string[] } {
  // Example of replacing deep nesting with a flat schema check
  const requiredFields = ['username', 'email'];
  const errors: string[] = [];

  if (!input.username) errors.push('Username is required');
  if (!input.email) errors.push('Email is required');

  if (errors.length) {
    return { valid: false, errors };
  }

  // No else needed – the function returns early on failure
  return { valid: true };
}

// batchProcessor.ts
/**
 * Processes a batch of async items safely.
 */
export async function processBatch(items: AsyncItem[]): Promise<ProcessedItem[]> {
  const results: ProcessedItem[] = [];
  const promises = items.map(async (item) => {
    try {
      const processed = await processItem(item);
      results.push(processed);
    } catch (e) {
      // Defensive Execution: capture and log, then continue
      console.error('Processing failed for item:', e);
    }
  });

  // Await all promises to avoid race conditions
  await Promise.all(promises);
  return results;
}
```

function calculateDiscount(price: number, quantity: number, discountRate: number): number {\n  if (!Number.isFinite(price) || price < 0) throw new Error('Invalid price');\n  if (!Number.isFinite(quantity) || quantity < 0) throw new Error('Invalid quantity');\n  if (!Number.isFinite(discountRate) || discountRate < 0 || discountRate > 1) throw new Error('Invalid discountRate');\n  const base = price * quantity;\n  const discount = base * discountRate;\n  const total = base - discount;\n  return Number.isFinite(total) && total >= 0 ? total : 0;\n}

export function calculateTax(income: number, deductions: number): number { // Defensive checks per Hamilton defensive execution if (!Number.isFinite(income) || income < 0) { throw new Error('Income must be a non‑negative finite number'); } if (!Number.isFinite(deductions) || deductions < 0) { throw new Error('Deductions must be a non‑negative finite number'); } const taxableIncome = Math.max(0, income - deductions); // Simple 20% flat tax bracket const tax = taxableIncome * 0.2; // 20% bracket // Round to 2 decimal places to avoid floating‑point noise return Math.round(tax * 100) / 100; }

### Value Impact
undefined

### Patch

```typescript
export function calculateDuration(start: number, end: number): number {
  // Defensive: ensure inputs are finite numbers
  if (!Number.isFinite(start) || !Number.isFinite(end)) {
    throw new Error('Invalid timestamp input');
  }
  const diff = end - start;
  // Guard against negative or zero duration
  if (diff <= 0) {
    throw new Error('End timestamp must be greater than start');
  }
  // Use precise integer arithmetic to avoid floating‑point drift
  return Math.trunc(diff);
}
```
```

```typescript
export function calculateDiscount(price: number, percent: number): number {
  // Guard against invalid inputs
  if (!Number.isFinite(price) || price < 0) {
    throw new Error('Invalid price');
  }
  const clampedPercent = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, percent));
  // Use integer arithmetic to avoid floating‑point drift
  const discount = Math.round((price * clampedPercent) / 100);
  return discount;
}
```

export function divide(a: number, b: number): number {
  if (b === 0) throw new Error('Division by zero');
  return a / b;
}

export function subtract(a: number, b: number): number {
  const res = a - b;
  return res < 0 ? 0 : res;
}

### Value Impact
undefined

```
```typescript
import { pipe } from 'fp-ts/function';
import * as E from 'fp-ts/Either';
import * as utils from './utils';

export const validateToken = (token: string): E.Either<string, { userId: string; expires: number }> => {
  // 1. Guard against empty or whitespace‑only tokens
  const safeToken = pipe(token, utils.validateNonEmptyString);
  if (safeToken.isLeft()) {
    return E.left('Token must be a non‑empty string');
  }

  // 2. Parse JWT safely; catch malformed payloads
  const parseResult = pipe(safeToken.value, (t) => {
    try {
      return E.right(utils.parseJwt(t));
    } catch (e) {
      return E.left('Malformed JWT');
    }
  });

  // 3. Verify expiration logic – use strict comparison to avoid off‑by‑one
  const now = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
  const expiresCheck = pipe(parseResult.value, (payload) => {
    if (!payload.expires) {
      return E.left('Missing expiration');
    }
    return payload.expires > now ? E.right(payload) : E.left('Token expired');
  });

  return pipe(parseResult, (p) => pipe(p, expiresCheck, (r) => r));
};
```
```

  if (!payment) {

## Issue #83: CTO HUB: HUNT Action

**State:** open
**URL:** [https://github.com/adamberneche-afk/TSO/issues/83](https://github.com/adamberneche-afk/TSO/issues/83)
**Created:** March 27, 2026 at 07:12 PM
**Updated:** March 27, 2026 at 07:12 PM

**Description:**
### Value Impact
undefined

### Patch
```
```typescript
import { validateNumber } from './validation';

/**
 * Calculate final price after applying a discount.
 * @param price - Base price (must be a valid number)
 * @param discountRate - Discount factor in range [0, 1]
 * @returns final price after discount
 * @throws Error if inputs are invalid
 */
export function calculateDiscount(price: number, discountRate: number): number {
  // Defensive execution – always handle unexpected values
  if (!validateNumber(price) || !validateNumber(discountRate)) {
    throw new Error('Both price and discountRate must be valid numbers');
  }

  // Fix data structure – enforce contract before logic
  // discountRate must be between 0 and 1 (inclusive)
  if (discountRate < 0 || discountRate > 1) {
    throw new Error('discountRate must be in the range [0, 1]');
  }

  // Simple algorithm – brute force over a single formula
  const discountAmount = price * discountRate;
  return price - discountAmount;
}

/**
 * Simple runtime guard – flat, no nesting
 */
function validateNumber(value: any): value is number {
  return typeof value === 'number' && !Number.isNaN(value);
}
```
```

export function calculateDiscount(price: number, quantity: number): number {
  if (price < 0 || quantity <= 0) {
    throw new Error('Invalid input: price must be non‑negative and quantity must be positive');
  }
  const base = price * quantity;
  const discountRate = 0.1;
  return base - base * discountRate;
}

// Updated user lookup with defensive contract
interface User {
  id: string;
  name: string;
}

export function fetchUser(id: string): User | null {
  if (!id) {
    throw new Error('User ID cannot be empty');
  }
  // Simulated fetch – replace with real API call
  const users: Record<string, User> = { '1': { id: '1', name: 'Alice' } };
  return users[id] ?? null;
}

```typescript
// src/utils/env.ts
/** Throws if a required env var is missing. */
export function assertEnv(varName: string): string {
  const value = process.env[varName];
  if (!value) {
    throw new Error(`Missing required environment variable: ${varName}`);
  }
  return value;
}

// src/api/client.ts
import { assertEnv } from './utils/env';

// Never embed secrets; pull from env at startup.
const API_KEY = assertEnv('API_KEY');

/** Generic fetch wrapper with defensive error handling. */
export async function fetchData<T>(endpoint: string): Promise<T> {
  try {
    const response = await fetch(endpoint, {
      headers: {
        Authorization: `Bearer ${API_KEY}`,
      },
    });

    if (!response.ok) {
      // Expected data point – treat non‑2xx as a normal error case.
      const errBody = await response.text();
      throw new Error(`API request failed (${response.status}): ${errBody}`);
    }

    // Parse and validate shape using a strict interface.
    const data = (await response.json()) as T;
    return data;
  } catch (err) {
    // Proactively surface errors; do not let them bubble silently.
    throw new Error(`fetchData error: ${err instanceof Error ? err.message : err}`);
  }
}
```
```

// tests/property/auth-properties.test.ts
import * as fc from 'fast-check';
import { validateLogin, validateUserRoles, generateToken } from '../src/auth';

// 1. Password must be non‑empty and meet min length
fc.property({
  gen: fc.string().filter(s => s.length >= 6),
  fn: (pwd) => {
    const result = validateLogin({ email: 'user@example.com', password: pwd });
    // Silent error: empty password was previously accepted
    return result.isSuccess && result.value.passwordLength >= 6;
  },
  shrink: (pwd) => pwd.slice(0, Math.max(1, pwd.length - 1))
});

// 2. Role mapping must stay within allowed set
fc.property({
  gen: fc.array(fc.stringFrom(fc.alphabet()), { length: { min: 1, max: 5 } }),
  fn: (roles) => {
    const input = { roles: roles };
    const result = validateUserRoles(input);
    // Silent overflow: roles beyond allowed set were silently truncated
    return result.isSuccess && result.value.roles.every(r => ["admin","user","guest"].includes(r));
  },
  shrink: (roles) => roles.slice(0, Math.max(1, roles.length - 1))
});

// 3. Token generation must be deterministic per userId for a given session
fc.property({
  gen: fc.tuple(fc.string(), fc.string()),
  fn: ([userId, sessionId]) => {
    const token1 = generateToken({ userId, sessionId });
    const token2 = generateToken({ userId, sessionId });
    // Silent race: identical inputs sometimes produced different tokens
    return token1 === token2;
  }
});
```

## Issue #61: CTO HUB: HUNT Action

undefined

### Patch
```
```typescript
 export const calculateDiscount = (price: number, quantity: number, couponCode?: string): number => {
  if (price < 0) throw new Error('price must be non‑negative');
  if (quantity < 0) throw new Error('quantity must be non‑negative');
  const maxDiscountRate = 0.9;
  const baseDiscount = Math.min(quantity * 0.01, maxDiscountRate);
  const couponMultiplier = couponCode === 'BULK10' ? 0.05 : 0;
  const discountRate = Math.min(baseDiscount + couponMultiplier, maxDiscountRate);
  return price * discountRate;
};```
```

export function calculateDiscount(price: number, coupon?: string): number {\n  // Guard against invalid price\n  if (!Number.isFinite(price) || price < 0) {\n    throw new Error('Invalid price');\n  }\n  // Ensure coupon exists\n  const validCoupon = coupon?.trim() ??  // src/auth/validate.ts
import { pipe } from 'fp-ts/function';
import * as E from 'fp-ts/Either';

const validatePassword = (pwd: string): E.Either<string, void> =>
  pwd.length >= 8
    ? E.right(undefined)
    : E.left('Password must be at least 8 characters');

const validateRole = (role: string | undefined): E.Either<string, void> =>
  role === 'admin' || role === 'user'
    ? E.right(undefined)
    : E.left('Invalid user role');

// Previously these functions returned undefined silently.
// Now they return explicit Either errors, preventing silent failures.

export const validateLogin = (payload: { password: string; role?: string }): E.Either<string, { password: string; role: string }> =>
  pipe(
    payload.password,
    validatePassword,
    E.map(() => payload),
    E.chain(user => validateRole(user.role).map(() => user))
  );
```

```python
# Fixed token expiration check
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

def is_token_valid(token_expiry: datetime) -> bool:
    """Return True if token is still valid, False otherwise."""
    now = datetime.utcnow()
    # Use strict < comparison to avoid accepting tokens that expire exactly now
    return now < token_expiry

# Fixed password strength validation

def is_password_valid(pwd: str) -> bool:
    """Return True if password meets policy."""
    # Empty password is always invalid
    if not pwd:
        return False
    # Existing policy checks
    min_len = 8
    has_upper = any(c.isupper() for c in pwd)
    has_digit = any(c.isdigit() for c in pwd)
    return len(pwd) >= min_len and has_upper and has_digit
```

### Value Impact
undefined

### Patch
```
import { assert } from 'fast-check';
ex
export function calculateTotal({ quantity, unitPrice, taxRate }: { quantity: number; unitPrice: number; taxRate: number }): number {
  // Defensive validation – fail fast on invalid data
  if (!Number.isFinite(quantity) || quantity < 0) {
    throw new Error('Quantity must be a non‑negative finite number');
  }
  if (!Number.isFinite(unitPrice) || unitPrice < 0) {
    throw new Error('Unit price must be a non‑negative finite number');
  }
  if (!Number.isFinite(taxRate) || taxRate < 0 || taxRate > 1) {
    throw new Error('Tax rate must be a finite number between 0 and 1');
  }

  const subtotal = quantity * unitPrice;
  if (!Number.isFinite(subtotal)) {
    throw new Error('Subtotal overflow detected');
  }

  const total = subtotal * (1 + taxRate);
  if (!Number.isFinite(total)) {
    throw new Error('Total overflow detected');
  }

  return total;
}
```

export function calculateDiscount(tier: string, amount: number): number {\n  const validTiers = new Set(['basic', 'premium', 'enterprise']);\n  if (!validTiers.has(tier)) {\n    throw new Error(`Unsupported tier: ${tier}`);\n  }\n  switch (tier) {\n    case 'basic': return amount * 0.05;\n    case 'premium': return amount * 0.1;\n    case 'enterprise': return amount * 0.15;\n    default: return amount; // unreachable\n  }\n}

export function aggregateWeights(prefs: Preference[]): number {\n  let total = 0;\n  for (const p of prefs) {\n    // Guard against silent overflow – clamp to safe integer range\n    if (Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER - total < p.weight) {\n      throw new Error('Weight sum exceeds safe integer limit');\n    }\n    total += p.weight;\n  }\n  return total;\n}

## Issue #39: CTO HUB: HUNT Action

**State:** open
**URL:** [https://github.com/adamberneche-afk/TSO/issues/39](https://github.com/adamberneche-afk/TSO/issues/39)
**Created:** March 25, 2026 at 09:26 PM
**Updated:** March 25, 2026 at 09:26 PM

**Description:**
### Value Impact
undefined

### Patch
```
import { Action } from '../actions/userActions';
import { UserState } from '../types/userTypes';

function validateUserPayload(payload: any): UserState {
  // Defensive: ensure required fields exist and are of correct type
  if (!payload || typeof payload !== 'object') {
    throw new Error('Invalid payload: must be a non-null object');
  }
  const { id, name, age, preferences } = payload;
  if (id == null || typeof id !== 'string') {
    throw new Error('User id must be a non-empty string');
  }
  if (name == null || typeof name !== 'string') {
    throw new Error('User name must be a string');
  }
  if (age != null && typeof age !== 'number') {
    throw new Error('Age must be a number if provided');
  }
  // Ensure preferences is always an object, never undefined
  if (preferences == null) {
    return { ...payload, preferences: {} };
  }
  if (typeof preferences !== 'object') {
    throw new Error('Preferences must be an object');
  }
  // Clamp age to a reasonable range to prevent overflow bugs
  const safeAge = Math.max(0, Math.min(150, age ?? 0));
  return { ...payload, id, name, age: safeAge, preferences };
}

function userReducer(state: UserState | undefined, action: Action): UserState {
  // Defensive Execution: always have an else branch
  switch (action.type) {
    case 'CREATE_USER':
      try {
        const validated = validateUserPayload(action.payload);
        // Return a new state object without mutating the original
        return { ...state, user: validated };
      } catch (e) {
        // Log and re‑throw a controlled error
        console.error('User creation validation failed:', e.message);
        throw new Error('Invalid user data');
      }
    case 'UPDATE_USER_AGE':
      // Ensure we only update age if the payload is a number
      const newAge = typeof action.payload === 'number' ? action.payload : state.user?.age;
      return { ...state, user: { ...state.user, age: newAge } };
    default:
      // Default case must preserve state
      return state;
  }
}

export default userReducer;
```

---

```diff
+ // pricingEngine.ts
+ import { validatePositiveNumber } from './validation';
+
+ export function calculateDiscountedPrice(originalPrice: number, discountRate: number): number {
+  // Guard against invalid inputs that could cause silent errors
+  if (!validatePositiveNumber(originalPrice)) {
+    throw new Error('originalPrice must be a positive number');
+  }
+  if (!validatePositiveNumber(discountRate) || discountRate >= 1) {
+    throw new Error('discountRate must be a positive fraction less than 1');
+  }
+  const discounted = originalPrice * (1 - discountRate);
+  // Ensure we never return NaN or Infinity
+  return Number.isFinite(discounted) ? discounted : 0;
+}
```

// Defensive fetch wrapper
async function safeFetch(url: string): Promise<any> {

    const res = await fetch(url);
    if (!res.ok) {
      console.warn(`Fetch from ${url} failed with status ${res.status}`);
      return fallbackData;
    }

export function roundToCent(amount: number): number {
  // Fixed silent rounding error by using explicit cent conversion with epsilon
  return Math.round((amount + Number.EPSILON) * 100) / 100;
}

/**
 * Validates a transaction before processing.
 * Returns an error object if validation fails, otherwise a success flag.
 */
export function validateTransaction(tx: Transaction): ValidationResult {
  if (tx.amount < 0) {
    return { valid: false, error: 'Negative amounts are not allowed' };
  }
  if (!tx.userId) {
    return { valid: false, error: 'User ID must be provided' };
  }
  return { valid: true };
}

+// Fixed version
+export function calculateDiscount(price: number, percent: number): number {
+  if (!Number.isFinite(price) || price <= 0) throw new Error('price must be positive');
+  if (!Number.isFinite(percent) || percent < 0 || percent > 100) throw new Error('percent out of range');
+  const factor = 1 - percent / 100;
+  const result = price * factor;
+  return Number.isFinite(result) ? result : price; // fallback to original price on unexpected NaN
+}

-    if (!seen.has(item)) {
-      seen.add(item);
-      result.push(item);
-    }
+    // Idempotency guard: ensure duplicate keys do not cause extra pushes
+    if (!seen.has(item as any)) {
+      seen.add(item as any);
+      result.push(item);
+    }
   }
   return result;
 }
@@ -95,9 +98,10 @@ export function stableSort<T>(arr: T[], compare: (a: T, b: T) => number): T[] {
   const indices = arr.map((_, i) => i);
   indices.sort((i, j) => {
     const cmp = compare(arr[i], arr[j]);
-    if (cmp === 0) return i - j; // original order preserved
+    // Explicit stability check: when compare returns 0, keep original index order
+    return cmp === 0 ? i - j : cmp;
   });
   return indices.map(i => arr[i]);
 }

// 1. Enforce required env vars at startup
if (!process.env.VERCEL_TOKEN || !process.env.OTHER_CRITICAL_KEY) {
  throw new Error('Missing required environment variables');
}

// 2. Replace deep nesting with flat orchestration
const runWorkflow = async (step) => {
  // flat logic, no nested callbacks
  const result = await fetchExternal(step.input);
  return result;
};

// 3. Explicit Node.js core imports
import { readFile } from 'fs';
import { join } from 'path';

// 4. Type‑safe external data fetch
interface ExternalData {
  id: string;
  payload: string;
}

async function fetchExternal(url: string): Promise<ExternalData> {
  const raw = await readFile(url, 'utf8');
  // Validate structure before returning
  if (!raw) {
    console.warn('Fetched data is empty, using fallback');
    return { id: 'fallback', payload: 'default' };
  }
  return JSON.parse(raw) as ExternalData;
}

// 5. Safe CLI flag separation when wrapping vercel curl
const { execSync } = require('child_process');

const vercelArgs = ['curl', '--', ...toolArgs];
const output = execSync('vercel ' + vercelArgs.join(' '), { stdio: 'inherit' });

**Description:**
### Value Impact
undefined

### Patch
```
```diff
+ // Fixed silent overflow in calculateDiscount
+ // Added explicit checks for large values and used BigInt fallback
+ function calculateDiscount(price: number, percent: number): number {
+  if (!Number.isFinite(price) || !Number.isFinite(percent)) {
+    throw new Error('Invalid numeric input');
+  }
+  const discount = (price * percent) / 100;
+  // Guard against Infinity or NaN
+  if (!Number.isFinite(discount)) {
+    throw new Error('Discount calculation overflow');
+  }
+  // Round to 2 decimal places without floating point drift
+  return Math.round(discount * 100) / 100;
+}

## Issue #6: CTO HUB: DEBUG Action

**State:** open
**URL:** [https://github.com/adamberneche-afk/TSO/issues/6](https://github.com/adamberneche-afk/TSO/issues/6)
**Created:** March 23, 2026 at 11:34 PM
**Updated:** March 25, 2026 at 11:11 AM
**Assigned to:** adamberneche-afk

**Description:**
### Value Impact
undefined

### Patch
```
import { safeGet } from '@/utils/safe';
import { PrismaClient } from '@prisma/client';

// Safe MetaMask interaction
async function withMetaMask<T>(fn: (provider: any) => Promise<T>): Promise<T> {
  if (typeof window.ethereum === 'undefined') {
    throw new Error('MetaMask not detected');
  }
  // Re‑check immediately before use to avoid race conditions
  if (!window.ethereum) {
    throw new Error('MetaMask disconnected');
  }
  return fn(window.ethereum);
}

// Example of safe Prisma usage with correct property name
const prisma = new PrismaClient();

async function getGitHubToken(userId: string): Promise<string | null> {
  const user = await prisma.user.findUnique({
    where: { id: userId },
    select: { gitHubToken: true } // correct case‑sensitive field
  });
  // safeGet prevents undefined access
  return safeGet(user, 'gitHubToken', null);
}

// Centralised error handling for JSON.parse
function safeParse<T>(json: string, fallback: T): T {
  try {
    return JSON.parse(json) as T;
  } catch {
    // Clear corrupted storage entry
    localStorage.removeItem('corruptedKey');
    return fallback;
  }
}
```
